Section: Does this plan provide Minimum Essential Coverage? [section_005] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Section: Does this plan meet Minimum Value Standards? [section_006] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

What is the overall deductible? -[TYPE]-> important_question
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. Preventive care and primary care services are covered before you meet your deductible.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_001
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[TYPE]-> important_question
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. $300 for prescription drug coverage and $300 for occupational therapy services.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_002
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[TYPE]-> important_question
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[ANSWER]-> For network providers $2,500 individual / $5,000 family; for out-of-network providers $4,000 individual / $8,000 family
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_003
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[TYPE]-> important_question
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[ANSWER]-> Copayments for certain services, premiums, balance-billed charges, and health care this plan doesn’t cover.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_004
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[TYPE]-> important_question

Specialist visit -[LIMITATIONS]-> Preauthorization is required. Failure to obtain preauthorization may result in a reduction in benefits by 50% of the total cost of the service.

Preventive care/screening/immunization -[NETWORK_COST]-> No charge for covered services
Preventive care/screening/immunization -[OUT_OF_NETWORK_COST]-> 40% coinsurance
Preventive care/screening/immunization -[LIMITATIONS]-> You may have to pay for services that aren’t preventive. Ask your provider if the services you need are preventive. Then check what your plan will pay for.

Specialty drugs (Tier 4) -[LIMITATIONS]-> Covers up to a 30-day supply (retail subscription); 31-90 day supply (mail order prescription).

Section: page_4.html [section_004] -[CONTENT]-> Your Grievance and Appeals Rights: There are agencies that can help if you have a complaint against your plan for a denial of a claim. This complaint is called a grievance or appeal. For more information about your rights, look at the explanation of benefits you will receive for that medical claim. Your plan documents also provide complete information to submit a claim appeal or a grievance for any reason to your plan. For more information about your rights, this notice, or assistance, contact: [insert applicable contact information from instructions].
Section: Does this plan provide Minimum Essential Coverage? [section_005] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Section: Does this plan meet Minimum Value Standards? [section_006] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

Section: About these Coverage Examples: [section_008] -[CONTENT]-> This is not a cost estimator. Treatments shown are just examples of how this plan might cover medical care. Focus on the cost sharing amounts (deductibles, copayments and coinsurance) and excluded services under the plan. Use this information to compare the portion of costs you might pay under different health plans. Please note these coverage examples are based on self-only coverage. What is the overall deductible? -[TYPE]-> important_question
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. Preventive care and primary care services are covered before you meet your deductible.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_001
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[TYPE]-> important_question
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. $300 for prescription drug coverage and $300 for occupational therapy services.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_002
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[TYPE]-> important_question
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[ANSWER]-> For network providers $2,500 individual / $5,000 family; for out-of-network providers $4,000 individual / $8,000 family
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_003
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[TYPE]-> important_question
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[ANSWER]-> Copayments for certain services, premiums, balance-billed charges, and health care this plan doesn’t cover.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_004
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[TYPE]-> important_question

Primary care visit to treat an injury or illness -[LIMITATIONS]-> None

Specialist visit -[OUT_OF_NETWORK_COST]-> 40% coinsurance
Specialist visit -[LIMITATIONS]-> Preauthorization is required. Failure to obtain preauthorization may result in a reduction in benefits by 50% of the total cost of the service.
Specialist visit -[REQUIRES_PREAUTH]-> true
Preventive care/screening/immunization -[NETWORK_COST]-> No charge for covered services
Preventive care/screening/immunization -[OUT_OF_NETWORK_COST]-> 40% coinsurance
Preventive care/screening/immunization -[LIMITATIONS]-> You may have to pay for services that aren’t preventive. Ask your provider if the services you need are preventive. Then check what your plan will pay for.

Imaging (CT/PET scans, MRIs) -[NETWORK_COST]-> $50 copay/test

Specialty drugs (Tier 4) -[OUT_OF_NETWORK_COST]-> 70% coinsurance
Specialty drugs (Tier 4) -[LIMITATIONS]-> Covers up to a 30-day supply (retail subscription); 31-90 day supply (mail order prescription).
Facility fee (e.g., ambulatory surgery center) -[NETWORK_COST]-> $100/day copay
Facility fee (e.g., ambulatory surgery center) -[OUT_OF_NETWORK_COST]-> 40% coinsurance
Facility fee (e.g., ambulatory surgery center) -[LIMITATIONS]-> Preauthorization is required. Failure to obtain preauthorization may result in a reduction in benefits by 50% of the total cost of the service. 50% coinsurance for anesthesia.

Section: page_4.html [section_004] -[CONTENT]-> Your Grievance and Appeals Rights: There are agencies that can help if you have a complaint against your plan for a denial of a claim. This complaint is called a grievance or appeal. For more information about your rights, look at the explanation of benefits you will receive for that medical claim. Your plan documents also provide complete information to submit a claim appeal or a grievance for any reason to your plan. For more information about your rights, this notice, or assistance, contact: [insert applicable contact information from instructions].
Section: Does this plan provide Minimum Essential Coverage? [section_005] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Section: Does this plan meet Minimum Value Standards? [section_006] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

Focus on the cost sharing amounts (deductibles, copayments and coinsurance) and excluded services under the plan. Use this information to compare the portion of costs you might pay under different health plans. Please note these coverage examples are based on self-only coverage. Your plan documents also provide complete information to submit a claim appeal or a grievance for any reason to your plan. For more information about your rights, this notice, or assistance, contact: [insert applicable contact information from instructions].
Section: Does this plan provide Minimum Essential Coverage? [section_005] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Section: Does this plan meet Minimum Value Standards? [section_006] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

Section: page_4.html [section_004] -[CONTENT]-> Your Grievance and Appeals Rights: There are agencies that can help if you have a complaint against your plan for a denial of a claim. This complaint is called a grievance or appeal. For more information about your rights, look at the explanation of benefits you will receive for that medical claim. Your plan documents also provide complete information to submit a claim appeal or a grievance for any reason to your plan. For more information about your rights, this notice, or assistance, contact: [insert applicable contact information from instructions].
Section: Does this plan provide Minimum Essential Coverage? [section_005] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Section: Does this plan meet Minimum Value Standards? [section_006] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

What is the overall deductible? -[QUESTION]-> What is the overall deductible?
What is the overall deductible? -[ANSWER]-> $500/Individual or $1,000/family
What is the overall deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Generally, you must pay all of the costs from providers up to the deductible amount before this plan begins to pay. If you have other family members on the policy, they have to meet their own individual deductible until the overall family deductible amount has been met.
What is the overall deductible? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_000
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[QUESTION]-> Are there services covered before you meet your deductible?
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. Preventive care and primary care services are covered before you meet your deductible.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan covers some items and services even if you haven’t yet met the annual deductible amount. But a copayment or coinsurance may apply. For example, this plan covers certain preventive services without cost-sharing and before you meet your deductible. See a list of covered preventive services at https://www.healthcare.gov/coverage/preventive-care-benefits/.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_001
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[QUESTION]-> Are there other deductibles for specific services?
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. $300 for prescription drug coverage and $300 for occupational therapy services.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> You must pay all of the costs for these services up to the specific deductible amount before this plan begins to pay for these services.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_002
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[QUESTION]-> What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan?
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[ANSWER]-> For network providers $2,500 individual / $5,000 family; for out-of-network providers $4,000 individual / $8,000 family
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> The out-of-pocket limit is the most you could pay in a year for covered services. If you have other family members in this plan, they have to meet their own out-of-pocket limits until the overall family out-of-pocket limit has been met.
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_003
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[QUESTION]-> What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit?
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[ANSWER]-> Copayments for certain services, premiums, balance-billed charges, and health care this plan doesn’t cover.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Even though you pay these expenses, they don’t count toward the out-of-pocket limit.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_004
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[QUESTION]-> Will you pay less if you use a network provider?
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. See www.[insert].com or call 1-800-[insert] for a list of network providers.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan uses a provider network. You will pay less if you use a provider in the plan’s network. You will pay the most if you use an out-of-network provider, and you might receive a bill from a provider for the difference between the provider’s charge and what your plan pays (a balance bill). Be aware, your network provider might use an out-of-network provider for some services (such as lab work). Check with your provider before you get services.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_005
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[QUESTION]-> Do you need a referral to see a specialist?
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[ANSWER]-> Yes.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan will pay some or all of the costs to see a specialist for covered services but only if you have a referral before you see the specialist.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[CHUNK_ID]-> iq_006

Section: Does this plan provide Minimum Essential Coverage? [section_005] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Section: Does this plan meet Minimum Value Standards? [section_006] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

HealthPlan -[PLAN_TYPE]-> Coverage for: Family | Plan Type: PPO
What is the overall deductible? -[QUESTION]-> What is the overall deductible?
What is the overall deductible? -[ANSWER]-> $500/Individual or $1,000/family
What is the overall deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Generally, you must pay all of the costs from providers up to the deductible amount before this plan begins to pay. If you have other family members on the policy, they have to meet their own individual deductible until the overall family deductible amount has been met.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[QUESTION]-> Are there services covered before you meet your deductible?
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. Preventive care and primary care services are covered before you meet your deductible.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan covers some items and services even if you haven’t yet met the annual deductible amount. But a copayment or coinsurance may apply. For example, this plan covers certain preventive services without cost-sharing and before you meet your deductible. See a list of covered preventive services at https://www.healthcare.gov/coverage/preventive-care-benefits/.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[QUESTION]-> Are there other deductibles for specific services?
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. $300 for prescription drug coverage and $300 for occupational therapy services.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> You must pay all of the costs for these services up to the specific deductible amount before this plan begins to pay for these services.
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[QUESTION]-> What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan?
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[ANSWER]-> For network providers $2,500 individual / $5,000 family; for out-of-network providers $4,000 individual / $8,000 family
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> The out-of-pocket limit is the most you could pay in a year for covered services. If you have other family members in this plan, they have to meet their own out-of-pocket limits until the overall family out-of-pocket limit has been met.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[QUESTION]-> What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit?
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[ANSWER]-> Copayments for certain services, premiums, balance-billed charges, and health care this plan doesn’t cover.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Even though you pay these expenses, they don’t count toward the out-of-pocket limit.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[QUESTION]-> Will you pay less if you use a network provider?
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. See www.[insert].com or call 1-800-[insert] for a list of network providers.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan uses a provider network. You will pay less if you use a provider in the plan’s network. You will pay the most if you use an out-of-network provider, and you might receive a bill from a provider for the difference between the provider’s charge and what your plan pays (a balance bill). Be aware, your network provider might use an out-of-network provider for some services (such as lab work). Check with your provider before you get services.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[QUESTION]-> Do you need a referral to see a specialist?
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[ANSWER]-> Yes.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan will pay some or all of the costs to see a specialist for covered services but only if you have a referral before you see the specialist.

Section: Does this plan provide Minimum Essential Coverage? [section_005] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Section: Does this plan meet Minimum Value Standards? [section_006] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

HealthPlan -[HAS_SECTION]-> Section: Mia’s Simple Fracture [section_010]
HealthPlan -[PLAN_TYPE]-> Coverage for: Family | Plan Type: PPO
What is the overall deductible? -[QUESTION]-> What is the overall deductible?
What is the overall deductible? -[ANSWER]-> $500/Individual or $1,000/family
What is the overall deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Generally, you must pay all of the costs from providers up to the deductible amount before this plan begins to pay. If you have other family members on the policy, they have to meet their own individual deductible until the overall family deductible amount has been met.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[QUESTION]-> Are there services covered before you meet your deductible?
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. Preventive care and primary care services are covered before you meet your deductible.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan covers some items and services even if you haven’t yet met the annual deductible amount. But a copayment or coinsurance may apply. For example, this plan covers certain preventive services without cost-sharing and before you meet your deductible. See a list of covered preventive services at https://www.healthcare.gov/coverage/preventive-care-benefits/.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[QUESTION]-> Are there other deductibles for specific services?
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. $300 for prescription drug coverage and $300 for occupational therapy services.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> You must pay all of the costs for these services up to the specific deductible amount before this plan begins to pay for these services.
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[QUESTION]-> What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan?
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[ANSWER]-> For network providers $2,500 individual / $5,000 family; for out-of-network providers $4,000 individual / $8,000 family
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> The out-of-pocket limit is the most you could pay in a year for covered services. If you have other family members in this plan, they have to meet their own out-of-pocket limits until the overall family out-of-pocket limit has been met.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[QUESTION]-> What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit?
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[ANSWER]-> Copayments for certain services, premiums, balance-billed charges, and health care this plan doesn’t cover.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Even though you pay these expenses, they don’t count toward the out-of-pocket limit.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[QUESTION]-> Will you pay less if you use a network provider?
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. See www.[insert].com or call 1-800-[insert] for a list of network providers.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan uses a provider network. You will pay less if you use a provider in the plan’s network. You will pay the most if you use an out-of-network provider, and you might receive a bill from a provider for the difference between the provider’s charge and what your plan pays (a balance bill). Be aware, your network provider might use an out-of-network provider for some services (such as lab work). Check with your provider before you get services.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[QUESTION]-> Do you need a referral to see a specialist?
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[ANSWER]-> Yes.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan will pay some or all of the costs to see a specialist for covered services but only if you have a referral before you see the specialist.
Primary care visit to treat an injury or illness | Network -[RAW]-> $35 copay/office visit and 20% coinsurance for other outpatient services; deductible does not apply
Primary care visit to treat an injury or illness | Network | Copay -[VALUE]-> $35 copay
Primary care visit to treat an injury or illness | Network | Coinsurance -[VALUE]-> 20%
Primary care visit to treat an injury or illness | OutOfNetwork -[RAW]-> 40% coinsurance
Primary care visit to treat an injury or illness | OutOfNetwork | Coinsurance -[VALUE]-> 40%
Specialist visit | Network -[RAW]-> $50 copay/visit
Specialist visit | Network | Copay -[VALUE]-> $50 copay
Specialist visit | OutOfNetwork -[RAW]-> 40% coinsurance
Specialist visit | OutOfNetwork | Coinsurance -[VALUE]-> 40%
Specialist visit | Limitation -[TEXT]-> Preauthorization is required. Failure to obtain preauthorization may result in a reduction in benefits by 50% of the total cost of the service.
Preventive care/screening/immunization | Network -[RAW]-> No charge for covered services
Preventive care/screening/immunization | OutOfNetwork -[RAW]-> 40% coinsurance
Preventive care/screening/immunization | OutOfNetwork | Coinsurance -[VALUE]-> 40%
Preventive care/screening/immunization | Limitation -[TEXT]-> You may have to pay for services that aren’t preventive. Ask your provider if the services you need are preventive. Then check what your plan will pay for.

Section: page_4.html [section_004] -[CONTENT]-> Your Grievance and Appeals Rights: There are agencies that can help if you have a complaint against your plan for a denial of a claim. This complaint is called a grievance or appeal. For more information about your rights, look at the explanation of benefits you will receive for that medical claim. Your plan documents also provide complete information to submit a claim appeal or a grievance for any reason to your plan. For more information about your rights, this notice, or assistance, contact: [insert applicable contact information from instructions].
Section: Does this plan provide Minimum Essential Coverage? [section_005] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Section: Does this plan meet Minimum Value Standards? [section_006] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

HealthPlan -[PLAN_TYPE]-> Coverage for: Family | Plan Type: PPO
What is the overall deductible? -[QUESTION]-> What is the overall deductible?
What is the overall deductible? -[ANSWER]-> $500/Individual or $1,000/family
What is the overall deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Generally, you must pay all of the costs from providers up to the deductible amount before this plan begins to pay. If you have other family members on the policy, they have to meet their own individual deductible until the overall family deductible amount has been met.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[QUESTION]-> Are there services covered before you meet your deductible?
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. Preventive care and primary care services are covered before you meet your deductible.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan covers some items and services even if you haven’t yet met the annual deductible amount. But a copayment or coinsurance may apply. For example, this plan covers certain preventive services without cost-sharing and before you meet your deductible. See a list of covered preventive services at https://www.healthcare.gov/coverage/preventive-care-benefits/.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[QUESTION]-> Are there other deductibles for specific services?
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. $300 for prescription drug coverage and $300 for occupational therapy services.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> You must pay all of the costs for these services up to the specific deductible amount before this plan begins to pay for these services.
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[QUESTION]-> What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan?
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[ANSWER]-> For network providers $2,500 individual / $5,000 family; for out-of-network providers $4,000 individual / $8,000 family
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> The out-of-pocket limit is the most you could pay in a year for covered services. If you have other family members in this plan, they have to meet their own out-of-pocket limits until the overall family out-of-pocket limit has been met.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[QUESTION]-> What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit?
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[ANSWER]-> Copayments for certain services, premiums, balance-billed charges, and health care this plan doesn’t cover.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Even though you pay these expenses, they don’t count toward the out-of-pocket limit.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[QUESTION]-> Will you pay less if you use a network provider?
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. See www.[insert].com or call 1-800-[insert] for a list of network providers.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan uses a provider network. You will pay less if you use a provider in the plan’s network. You will pay the most if you use an out-of-network provider, and you might receive a bill from a provider for the difference between the provider’s charge and what your plan pays (a balance bill). Be aware, your network provider might use an out-of-network provider for some services (such as lab work). Check with your provider before you get services.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[QUESTION]-> Do you need a referral to see a specialist?
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[ANSWER]-> Yes.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan will pay some or all of the costs to see a specialist for covered services but only if you have a referral before you see the specialist.

Section: Does this plan provide Minimum Essential Coverage? [section_005] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Section: Does this plan meet Minimum Value Standards? [section_006] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

HealthPlan -[HAS_SECTION]-> Section: Mia’s Simple Fracture [section_010]
HealthPlan -[PLAN_TYPE]-> Coverage for: Family | Plan Type: PPO
What is the overall deductible? -[QUESTION]-> What is the overall deductible?
What is the overall deductible? -[ANSWER]-> $500/Individual or $1,000/family
What is the overall deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Generally, you must pay all of the costs from providers up to the deductible amount before this plan begins to pay. If you have other family members on the policy, they have to meet their own individual deductible until the overall family deductible amount has been met.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[QUESTION]-> Are there services covered before you meet your deductible?
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. Preventive care and primary care services are covered before you meet your deductible.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan covers some items and services even if you haven’t yet met the annual deductible amount. But a copayment or coinsurance may apply. For example, this plan covers certain preventive services without cost-sharing and before you meet your deductible. See a list of covered preventive services at https://www.healthcare.gov/coverage/preventive-care-benefits/.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[QUESTION]-> Are there other deductibles for specific services?
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. $300 for prescription drug coverage and $300 for occupational therapy services.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> You must pay all of the costs for these services up to the specific deductible amount before this plan begins to pay for these services.
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[QUESTION]-> What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan?
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[ANSWER]-> For network providers $2,500 individual / $5,000 family; for out-of-network providers $4,000 individual / $8,000 family
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> The out-of-pocket limit is the most you could pay in a year for covered services. If you have other family members in this plan, they have to meet their own out-of-pocket limits until the overall family out-of-pocket limit has been met.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[QUESTION]-> What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit?
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[ANSWER]-> Copayments for certain services, premiums, balance-billed charges, and health care this plan doesn’t cover.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Even though you pay these expenses, they don’t count toward the out-of-pocket limit.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[QUESTION]-> Will you pay less if you use a network provider?
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. See www.[insert].com or call 1-800-[insert] for a list of network providers.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan uses a provider network. You will pay less if you use a provider in the plan’s network. You will pay the most if you use an out-of-network provider, and you might receive a bill from a provider for the difference between the provider’s charge and what your plan pays (a balance bill). Be aware, your network provider might use an out-of-network provider for some services (such as lab work). Check with your provider before you get services.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[QUESTION]-> Do you need a referral to see a specialist?
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[ANSWER]-> Yes.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan will pay some or all of the costs to see a specialist for covered services but only if you have a referral before you see the specialist.

Section: page_4.html [section_004] -[CONTENT]-> Your Grievance and Appeals Rights: There are agencies that can help if you have a complaint against your plan for a denial of a claim. This complaint is called a grievance or appeal. For more information about your rights, look at the explanation of benefits you will receive for that medical claim. Your plan documents also provide complete information to submit a claim appeal or a grievance for any reason to your plan. For more information about your rights, this notice, or assistance, contact: [insert applicable contact information from instructions].
Section: Does this plan provide Minimum Essential Coverage? [section_005] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Section: Does this plan meet Minimum Value Standards? [section_006] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

What is the overall deductible? -[QUESTION]-> What is the overall deductible?
What is the overall deductible? -[ANSWER]-> $500/Individual or $1,000/family
What is the overall deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Generally, you must pay all of the costs from providers up to the deductible amount before this plan begins to pay. If you have other family members on the policy, they have to meet their own individual deductible until the overall family deductible amount has been met.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[QUESTION]-> Are there services covered before you meet your deductible?
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. Preventive care and primary care services are covered before you meet your deductible.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan covers some items and services even if you haven’t yet met the annual deductible amount. But a copayment or coinsurance may apply. For example, this plan covers certain preventive services without cost-sharing and before you meet your deductible. See a list of covered preventive services at https://www.healthcare.gov/coverage/preventive-care-benefits/.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[QUESTION]-> Are there other deductibles for specific services?
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. $300 for prescription drug coverage and $300 for occupational therapy services.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> You must pay all of the costs for these services up to the specific deductible amount before this plan begins to pay for these services.
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[QUESTION]-> What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan?
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[ANSWER]-> For network providers $2,500 individual / $5,000 family; for out-of-network providers $4,000 individual / $8,000 family
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> The out-of-pocket limit is the most you could pay in a year for covered services. If you have other family members in this plan, they have to meet their own out-of-pocket limits until the overall family out-of-pocket limit has been met.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[QUESTION]-> What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit?
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[ANSWER]-> Copayments for certain services, premiums, balance-billed charges, and health care this plan doesn’t cover.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Even though you pay these expenses, they don’t count toward the out-of-pocket limit.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[QUESTION]-> Will you pay less if you use a network provider?
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. See www.[insert].com or call 1-800-[insert] for a list of network providers.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan uses a provider network. You will pay less if you use a provider in the plan’s network. You will pay the most if you use an out-of-network provider, and you might receive a bill from a provider for the difference between the provider’s charge and what your plan pays (a balance bill). Be aware, your network provider might use an out-of-network provider for some services (such as lab work). Check with your provider before you get services.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[QUESTION]-> Do you need a referral to see a specialist?
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[ANSWER]-> Yes.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan will pay some or all of the costs to see a specialist for covered services but only if you have a referral before you see the specialist.

Section: Does this plan provide Minimum Essential Coverage? [section_005] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Section: Does this plan meet Minimum Value Standards? [section_006] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

HealthPlan -[PLAN_TYPE]-> Coverage for: Family | Plan Type: PPO
What is the overall deductible? -[QUESTION]-> What is the overall deductible?
What is the overall deductible? -[ANSWER]-> $500/Individual or $1,000/family
What is the overall deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Generally, you must pay all of the costs from providers up to the deductible amount before this plan begins to pay. If you have other family members on the policy, they have to meet their own individual deductible until the overall family deductible amount has been met.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[QUESTION]-> Are there services covered before you meet your deductible?
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. Preventive care and primary care services are covered before you meet your deductible.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan covers some items and services even if you haven’t yet met the annual deductible amount. But a copayment or coinsurance may apply. For example, this plan covers certain preventive services without cost-sharing and before you meet your deductible. See a list of covered preventive services at https://www.healthcare.gov/coverage/preventive-care-benefits/.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[QUESTION]-> Are there other deductibles for specific services?
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. $300 for prescription drug coverage and $300 for occupational therapy services.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> You must pay all of the costs for these services up to the specific deductible amount before this plan begins to pay for these services.
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[QUESTION]-> What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan?
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[ANSWER]-> For network providers $2,500 individual / $5,000 family; for out-of-network providers $4,000 individual / $8,000 family
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> The out-of-pocket limit is the most you could pay in a year for covered services. If you have other family members in this plan, they have to meet their own out-of-pocket limits until the overall family out-of-pocket limit has been met.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[QUESTION]-> What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit?
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[ANSWER]-> Copayments for certain services, premiums, balance-billed charges, and health care this plan doesn’t cover.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Even though you pay these expenses, they don’t count toward the out-of-pocket limit.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[QUESTION]-> Will you pay less if you use a network provider?
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. See www.[insert].com or call 1-800-[insert] for a list of network providers.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan uses a provider network. You will pay less if you use a provider in the plan’s network. You will pay the most if you use an out-of-network provider, and you might receive a bill from a provider for the difference between the provider’s charge and what your plan pays (a balance bill). Be aware, your network provider might use an out-of-network provider for some services (such as lab work). Check with your provider before you get services.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[QUESTION]-> Do you need a referral to see a specialist?
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[ANSWER]-> Yes.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan will pay some or all of the costs to see a specialist for covered services but only if you have a referral before you see the specialist.

Section: Does this plan provide Minimum Essential Coverage? [section_005] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Section: Does this plan meet Minimum Value Standards? [section_006] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

Use this information to compare the portion of costs you might pay under different health plans. Please note these coverage examples are based on self-only coverage. HealthPlan -[HAS_SECTION]-> Section: Mia’s Simple Fracture [section_010]
HealthPlan -[PLAN_TYPE]-> Coverage for: Family | Plan Type: PPO
What is the overall deductible? -[QUESTION]-> What is the overall deductible?
What is the overall deductible? -[ANSWER]-> $500/Individual or $1,000/family
What is the overall deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Generally, you must pay all of the costs from providers up to the deductible amount before this plan begins to pay. If you have other family members on the policy, they have to meet their own individual deductible until the overall family deductible amount has been met.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[QUESTION]-> Are there services covered before you meet your deductible?
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. Preventive care and primary care services are covered before you meet your deductible.
Are there services covered before you meet your deductible? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan covers some items and services even if you haven’t yet met the annual deductible amount. But a copayment or coinsurance may apply. For example, this plan covers certain preventive services without cost-sharing and before you meet your deductible. See a list of covered preventive services at https://www.healthcare.gov/coverage/preventive-care-benefits/.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[QUESTION]-> Are there other deductibles for specific services?
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. $300 for prescription drug coverage and $300 for occupational therapy services.
Are there other deductibles for specific services? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> You must pay all of the costs for these services up to the specific deductible amount before this plan begins to pay for these services.
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[QUESTION]-> What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan?
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[ANSWER]-> For network providers $2,500 individual / $5,000 family; for out-of-network providers $4,000 individual / $8,000 family
What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> The out-of-pocket limit is the most you could pay in a year for covered services. If you have other family members in this plan, they have to meet their own out-of-pocket limits until the overall family out-of-pocket limit has been met.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[QUESTION]-> What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit?
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[ANSWER]-> Copayments for certain services, premiums, balance-billed charges, and health care this plan doesn’t cover.
What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Even though you pay these expenses, they don’t count toward the out-of-pocket limit.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[QUESTION]-> Will you pay less if you use a network provider?
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[ANSWER]-> Yes. See www.[insert].com or call 1-800-[insert] for a list of network providers.
Will you pay less if you use a network provider? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan uses a provider network. You will pay less if you use a provider in the plan’s network. You will pay the most if you use an out-of-network provider, and you might receive a bill from a provider for the difference between the provider’s charge and what your plan pays (a balance bill). Be aware, your network provider might use an out-of-network provider for some services (such as lab work). Check with your provider before you get services.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[QUESTION]-> Do you need a referral to see a specialist?
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[ANSWER]-> Yes.
Do you need a referral to see a specialist? -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan will pay some or all of the costs to see a specialist for covered services but only if you have a referral before you see the specialist.

Section: page_4.html [section_004] -[CONTENT]-> Your Grievance and Appeals Rights: There are agencies that can help if you have a complaint against your plan for a denial of a claim. This complaint is called a grievance or appeal. For more information about your rights, look at the explanation of benefits you will receive for that medical claim. Your plan documents also provide complete information to submit a claim appeal or a grievance for any reason to your plan. For more information about your rights, this notice, or assistance, contact: [insert applicable contact information from instructions].
Section: Does this plan provide Minimum Essential Coverage? [section_005] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Section: Does this plan meet Minimum Value Standards? [section_006] -[CONTENT]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

HealthPlan -[PLAN_TYPE]-> Coverage for: Family | Plan Type: PPO
Overall Deductible -[VALUE]-> $500/Individual or $1,000/family
Overall Deductible -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Generally, you must pay all of the costs from providers up to the deductible amount before this plan begins to pay. If you have other family members on the policy, they have to meet their own individual deductible until the overall family deductible amount has been met.
Overall Deductible -[QUESTION]-> What is the overall deductible?
Services Before Deductible -[VALUE]-> Yes. Preventive care and primary care services are covered before you meet your deductible.
Services Before Deductible -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan covers some items and services even if you haven’t yet met the annual deductible amount. But a copayment or coinsurance may apply. For example, this plan covers certain preventive services without cost-sharing and before you meet your deductible. See a list of covered preventive services at https://www.healthcare.gov/coverage/preventive-care-benefits/.
Services Before Deductible -[QUESTION]-> Are there services covered before you meet your deductible?
Service Specific Deductibles -[VALUE]-> Yes. $300 for prescription drug coverage and $300 for occupational therapy services.
Service Specific Deductibles -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> You must pay all of the costs for these services up to the specific deductible amount before this plan begins to pay for these services.
Service Specific Deductibles -[QUESTION]-> Are there other deductibles for specific services?
Out-of-Pocket Limit -[VALUE]-> For network providers $2,500 individual / $5,000 family; for out-of-network providers $4,000 individual / $8,000 family
Out-of-Pocket Limit -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> The out-of-pocket limit is the most you could pay in a year for covered services. If you have other family members in this plan, they have to meet their own out-of-pocket limits until the overall family out-of-pocket limit has been met.
Out-of-Pocket Limit -[QUESTION]-> What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan?
Out-of-Pocket Exclusions -[VALUE]-> Copayments for certain services, premiums, balance-billed charges, and health care this plan doesn’t cover.
Out-of-Pocket Exclusions -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Even though you pay these expenses, they don’t count toward the out-of-pocket limit.
Out-of-Pocket Exclusions -[QUESTION]-> What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit?
Network Provider Benefit -[VALUE]-> Yes. See www.[insert].com or call 1-800-[insert] for a list of network providers.
Network Provider Benefit -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan uses a provider network. You will pay less if you use a provider in the plan’s network. You will pay the most if you use an out-of-network provider, and you might receive a bill from a provider for the difference between the provider’s charge and what your plan pays (a balance bill). Be aware, your network provider might use an out-of-network provider for some services (such as lab work). Check with your provider before you get services.
Network Provider Benefit -[QUESTION]-> Will you pay less if you use a network provider?
Specialist Referral Requirement -[VALUE]-> Yes.
Specialist Referral Requirement -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan will pay some or all of the costs to see a specialist for covered services but only if you have a referral before you see the specialist.
Specialist Referral Requirement -[QUESTION]-> Do you need a referral to see a specialist?
Grievance and Appeals Rights -[SUMMARY]-> Your Grievance and Appeals Rights: There are agencies that can help if you have a complaint against your plan for a denial of a claim. This complaint is called a grievance or appeal. For more information about your rights, look at the explanation of benefits you will receive for that medical claim. Your plan documents also provide complete information to submit a claim appeal or a grievance for any reason to your plan. For more information about your rights, this notice, or assistance, contact: [insert applicable contact information from instructions].
Minimum Essential Coverage -[SUMMARY]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Minimum Value Standards -[SUMMARY]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

HealthPlan -[PLAN_TYPE]-> Coverage for: Family | Plan Type: PPO
Overall Deductible -[VALUE]-> $500/Individual or $1,000/family
Overall Deductible -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Generally, you must pay all of the costs from providers up to the deductible amount before this plan begins to pay. If you have other family members on the policy, they have to meet their own individual deductible until the overall family deductible amount has been met.
Overall Deductible -[QUESTION]-> What is the overall deductible?
Services Before Deductible -[VALUE]-> Yes. Preventive care and primary care services are covered before you meet your deductible.
Services Before Deductible -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan covers some items and services even if you haven’t yet met the annual deductible amount. But a copayment or coinsurance may apply. For example, this plan covers certain preventive services without cost-sharing and before you meet your deductible. See a list of covered preventive services at https://www.healthcare.gov/coverage/preventive-care-benefits/.
Services Before Deductible -[QUESTION]-> Are there services covered before you meet your deductible?
Service Specific Deductibles -[VALUE]-> Yes. $300 for prescription drug coverage and $300 for occupational therapy services.
Service Specific Deductibles -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> You must pay all of the costs for these services up to the specific deductible amount before this plan begins to pay for these services.
Service Specific Deductibles -[QUESTION]-> Are there other deductibles for specific services?
Out-of-Pocket Limit -[VALUE]-> For network providers $2,500 individual / $5,000 family; for out-of-network providers $4,000 individual / $8,000 family
Out-of-Pocket Limit -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> The out-of-pocket limit is the most you could pay in a year for covered services. If you have other family members in this plan, they have to meet their own out-of-pocket limits until the overall family out-of-pocket limit has been met.
Out-of-Pocket Limit -[QUESTION]-> What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan?
Out-of-Pocket Exclusions -[VALUE]-> Copayments for certain services, premiums, balance-billed charges, and health care this plan doesn’t cover.
Out-of-Pocket Exclusions -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Even though you pay these expenses, they don’t count toward the out-of-pocket limit.
Out-of-Pocket Exclusions -[QUESTION]-> What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit?
Network Provider Benefit -[VALUE]-> Yes. See www.[insert].com or call 1-800-[insert] for a list of network providers.
Network Provider Benefit -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan uses a provider network. You will pay less if you use a provider in the plan’s network. You will pay the most if you use an out-of-network provider, and you might receive a bill from a provider for the difference between the provider’s charge and what your plan pays (a balance bill). Be aware, your network provider might use an out-of-network provider for some services (such as lab work). Check with your provider before you get services.
Network Provider Benefit -[QUESTION]-> Will you pay less if you use a network provider?
Specialist Referral Requirement -[VALUE]-> Yes.
Specialist Referral Requirement -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan will pay some or all of the costs to see a specialist for covered services but only if you have a referral before you see the specialist.
Specialist Referral Requirement -[QUESTION]-> Do you need a referral to see a specialist?
Grievance and Appeals Rights -[SUMMARY]-> Your Grievance and Appeals Rights: There are agencies that can help if you have a complaint against your plan for a denial of a claim. This complaint is called a grievance or appeal. For more information about your rights, look at the explanation of benefits you will receive for that medical claim. Your plan documents also provide complete information to submit a claim appeal or a grievance for any reason to your plan. For more information about your rights, this notice, or assistance, contact: [insert applicable contact information from instructions].
Minimum Essential Coverage -[SUMMARY]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Minimum Value Standards -[SUMMARY]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.

HealthPlan -[OFFERS_WELLNESS_PROGRAM_SAVINGS]-> Wellness Program Cost Reduction Notice
HealthPlan -[PLAN_TYPE]-> Coverage for: Family | Plan Type: PPO
Overall Deductible -[VALUE]-> $500/Individual or $1,000/family
Overall Deductible -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Generally, you must pay all of the costs from providers up to the deductible amount before this plan begins to pay. If you have other family members on the policy, they have to meet their own individual deductible until the overall family deductible amount has been met.
Overall Deductible -[QUESTION]-> What is the overall deductible?
Services Before Deductible -[VALUE]-> Yes. Preventive care and primary care services are covered before you meet your deductible.
Services Before Deductible -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan covers some items and services even if you haven’t yet met the annual deductible amount. But a copayment or coinsurance may apply. For example, this plan covers certain preventive services without cost-sharing and before you meet your deductible. See a list of covered preventive services at https://www.healthcare.gov/coverage/preventive-care-benefits/.
Services Before Deductible -[QUESTION]-> Are there services covered before you meet your deductible?
Service Specific Deductibles -[VALUE]-> Yes. $300 for prescription drug coverage and $300 for occupational therapy services.
Service Specific Deductibles -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> You must pay all of the costs for these services up to the specific deductible amount before this plan begins to pay for these services.
Service Specific Deductibles -[QUESTION]-> Are there other deductibles for specific services?
Out-of-Pocket Limit -[VALUE]-> For network providers $2,500 individual / $5,000 family; for out-of-network providers $4,000 individual / $8,000 family
Out-of-Pocket Limit -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> The out-of-pocket limit is the most you could pay in a year for covered services. If you have other family members in this plan, they have to meet their own out-of-pocket limits until the overall family out-of-pocket limit has been met.
Out-of-Pocket Limit -[QUESTION]-> What is the out-of-pocket limit for this plan?
Out-of-Pocket Exclusions -[VALUE]-> Copayments for certain services, premiums, balance-billed charges, and health care this plan doesn’t cover.
Out-of-Pocket Exclusions -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> Even though you pay these expenses, they don’t count toward the out-of-pocket limit.
Out-of-Pocket Exclusions -[QUESTION]-> What is not included in the out-of-pocket limit?
Network Provider Benefit -[VALUE]-> Yes. See www.[insert].com or call 1-800-[insert] for a list of network providers.
Network Provider Benefit -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan uses a provider network. You will pay less if you use a provider in the plan’s network. You will pay the most if you use an out-of-network provider, and you might receive a bill from a provider for the difference between the provider’s charge and what your plan pays (a balance bill). Be aware, your network provider might use an out-of-network provider for some services (such as lab work). Check with your provider before you get services.
Network Provider Benefit -[QUESTION]-> Will you pay less if you use a network provider?
Specialist Referral Requirement -[VALUE]-> Yes.
Specialist Referral Requirement -[WHY_IT_MATTERS]-> This plan will pay some or all of the costs to see a specialist for covered services but only if you have a referral before you see the specialist.
Specialist Referral Requirement -[QUESTION]-> Do you need a referral to see a specialist?
Grievance and Appeals Rights -[SUMMARY]-> Your Grievance and Appeals Rights: There are agencies that can help if you have a complaint against your plan for a denial of a claim. This complaint is called a grievance or appeal. For more information about your rights, look at the explanation of benefits you will receive for that medical claim. Your plan documents also provide complete information to submit a claim appeal or a grievance for any reason to your plan. For more information about your rights, this notice, or assistance, contact: [insert applicable contact information from instructions].
Minimum Essential Coverage -[SUMMARY]-> Yes. If you don't have Minimum Essential Coverage for a month under this plan or under other coverage, you'll have to make a payment when you file your tax return unless you qualify for an exemption from the requirement that you have health coverage for that month.
Minimum Value Standards -[SUMMARY]-> Yes. If your plan doesn't meet the Minimum Value Standards, you may be eligible for a premium tax credit to help you pay for a plan through the Marketplace.
Language Assistance Services -[SUMMARY]-> [Spanish (Español): Para obtener asistencia en Español, llame al [insert telephone number].] [Tagalog (Tagalog): Kung kailangan ninyo ang tulong sa Tagalog tumawag sa [insert telephone number].] [Chinese (中文): 如果需要中文的帮助，请拨打这个号码 [insert telephone number].] [Navajo (Dine): Dinek'ehgo shika at'ohwol ninisingo, kwijjigo holne' [insert telephone number].] —To see examples of how this plan might cover costs for a sample medical situation, see the next section.—
Health Coverage Cost Examples -[SUMMARY]-> This is not a cost estimator. Treatments shown are just examples of how this plan might cover medical care. Your actual costs will be different depending on the actual care you receive, the prices your providers charge, and many other factors. Focus on the cost sharing amounts (deductibles, copayments and coinsurance) and excluded services under the plan. Use this information to compare the portion of costs you might pay under different health plans. Please note these coverage examples are based on self-only coverage.
